<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/and" class="extiw" title="w:and">and</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/and" class="extiw" title="w:and">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stressed</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">ănd</span>, <span class="AHD enPR">ĕnd</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ænd/</span>, <span class="IPA">/ɛnd/</span></li>
<li><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r50165410">.mw-parser-output .k-player .k-attribution{visibility:hidden}</style><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: bottom; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">Audio (US)</td><td class="audiofile"><audio id="mwe_player_0" controls="" preload="none" width="175" style="width:175px;" data-durationhint="1" data-mwtitle="en-us-and.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/2/26/En-us-and.ogg" type="audio/ogg; codecs=&quot;vorbis&quot;" data-title="Original Ogg file (134 kbps)" data-shorttitle="Ogg source" data-width="0" data-height="0" data-bandwidth="133872" /><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/2/26/En-us-and.ogg/En-us-and.ogg.mp3" type="audio/mpeg" data-title="MP3" data-shorttitle="MP3" data-transcodekey="mp3" data-width="0" data-height="0" /></audio></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:en-us-and.ogg" title="File:en-us-and.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">unstressed</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">ən(d)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ənd/</span>, <span class="IPA">/ən/</span>, <span class="IPA">/ɛn/</span>, <span class="IPA">/ɛnd/</span>, <span class="IPA">/n̩d/</span>, <span class="IPA">/n̩/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/and#Middle_English" title="and">and</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/an#Middle_English" title="an">an</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/and#Old_English" title="and">and</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/ond#Old_English" title="ond">ond</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/end#Old_English" title="end">end</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/andi" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/andi">*andi</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/an%C3%BEi&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anþi (page does not exist)">*anþi</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82%C3%A9nti" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂énti">*h₂énti</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">facing opposite, near, in front of, before</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href="/wiki/an#Scots" title="an">an</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:North Frisian language">North Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frr"><a href="/wiki/en#North_Frisian" title="en">en</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href="/wiki/en#West_Frisian" title="en">en</a>, <a href="/wiki/in#West_Frisian" title="in">in</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href="/wiki/un#Low_German" title="un">un</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/en#Dutch" title="en">en</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/und#German" title="und">und</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/end#Danish" title="end">end</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">but</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/wiki/%C3%A4n#Swedish" title="än">än</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">yet, but</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href="/wiki/enn#Icelandic" title="enn">enn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">still, yet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq"><a href="/wiki/edhe#Albanian" title="edhe">edhe</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">and</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%C3%AAnde&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ênde (page does not exist)">ênde</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=%C3%AAnne&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="ênne (page does not exist)">ênne</a></i>), <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq"><a href="/wiki/ende#Albanian" title="ende">ende</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">still, yet, therefore</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/ante#Latin" title="ante">ante</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">opposite, in front of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%E1%BC%80%CE%BD%CF%84%CE%AF#Ancient_Greek" title="ἀντί">ἀντί</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">antí</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">opposite, facing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/an%27#English" title="an&#39;">an'</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/%27n%27#English" title="&#39;n&#39;">'n'</a></span> (<span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/n#English" title="n">n</a></span>)</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Conjunction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">and</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>As a coordinating conjunction; expressing two elements to be taken together or in addition to each other.
<ol><li>Used simply to connect two noun phrases, adjectives or adverbs. <span class="defdate">[from 8<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>c. 1430</b> (reprinted <b>1888</b>), Thomas Austin, ed., <i>Two Fifteenth-century Cookery-books. Harleian ms. 279 (ab. 1430), &amp; Harl. ms. 4016 (ab. 1450), with Extracts from Ashmole ms. 1429, Laud ms. 553, &amp; Douce ms. 55</i> [Early English Text Society, Original Series; 91], London: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Routledge" class="extiw" title="w:Routledge">N. Trübner &amp; Co.</a> for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Early_English_Text_Society" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Early English Text Society">Early English Text Society</a>, volume I, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Online_Computer_Library_Center" class="extiw" title="w:Online Computer Library Center">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/374760">374760</a></small>, page 11:
<dl><dd>Soupes dorye. — Take gode almaunde mylke <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span> caste þher-to Safroun <b>an</b> Salt <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span></dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <b>1596–1598</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Merchant_of_Venice" class="extiw" title="w:The Merchant of Venice">The Merchant of Venice</a>”, in  <cite>Mr. William Shakespeares Comedies, Histories, &amp; Tragedies: Published According to the True Originall Copies</cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London&#58; <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Printed by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act V, scene i]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Sweet lady, you have given me life <b>and</b> living; <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. Newly Translated out of the Originall Tongues: &amp; with the Former Translations Diligently Compared and Reuised, by His Maiesties Speciall Comandement. Appointed to be Read in Churches.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_James_Version" class="extiw" title="w:King James Version">King James Version</a>), London&#58; <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Imprinted at London by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barker_(printer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barker (printer)">Robert Barker</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="printer to the Kings Most Excellent Maiestie.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/964384981">964384981</a></small>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Genesis" class="extiw" title="w:Book of Genesis">Genesis</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.kingjamesbibleonline.org/1611_Genesis-Chapter-1/#1">1&#58;1</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In the beginning God created the heaven <b>and</b> the earth.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1817</b> December,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jane_Austen" class="extiw" title="w:Jane Austen">[Jane Austen]</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persuasion_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:Persuasion (novel)">Persuasion</a></cite>&#59; published in  <cite>Northanger Abbey: And Persuasion.<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="&#91;...&#93; With a Biographical Notice of the Author. In Four Volumes.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite>, volume <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(please specify |volume=I to IV)</span>, London&#58; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Murray_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:John Murray (publisher)">John Murray</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Albemarle-Street">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, 1818, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/318384910">318384910</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">as for Mrs. Smith, she had claims of various kinds to recommend her quickly <b>and</b> permanently.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2011</b>, Mark Townsend, <i>The Guardian</i>, 5 November:
<dl><dd>‘The UKBA has some serious explaining to do if it is routinely carrying out such abusive <b>and</b> unlawful inspections.’</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Simply connecting two clauses or sentences. <span class="defdate">[from 8<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1991</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jung_Chang" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jung Chang">Jung Chang</a>, <i>Wild Swans</i>:
<dl><dd>When she saw several boys carrying a huge wooden case full of porcelain, she mumbled to Jinming that she was going to have a look, <b>and</b> left the room.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2011</b>, Helena Smith &amp; Tom Kington, <i>The Guardian</i>, 5 November:
<dl><dd>"Consensus is essential for the country," he said, adding that he was not "tied" to his post <b>and</b> was willing to step aside.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Introducing a clause or sentence which follows on in time or consequence from the first. <span class="defdate">[from 9<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1996</b>, David Beasley, <i>Chocolate for the Poor</i>:
<dl><dd>‘But if you think you can get it, Christian, you're a fool. Set one foot upcountry <b>and</b> I'll kill you.’</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2004</b>, Will Buckley, <i>The Observer</i>:, 22 August:
<dl><dd>One more error <b>and</b> all the good work she had done on Friday would be for nought.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/yet" title="yet">Yet</a>; <a href="/wiki/but" title="but">but</a>. <span class="defdate">[10<sup>th</sup>-17<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. Newly Translated out of the Originall Tongues: &amp; with the Former Translations Diligently Compared and Reuised, by His Maiesties Speciall Comandement. Appointed to be Read in Churches.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_James_Version" class="extiw" title="w:King James Version">King James Version</a>), London&#58; <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Imprinted at London by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barker_(printer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barker (printer)">Robert Barker</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="printer to the Kings Most Excellent Maiestie.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/964384981">964384981</a></small>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gospel_of_Matthew" class="extiw" title="w:Gospel of Matthew">Matthew</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.kingjamesbibleonline.org/1611_Matthew-Chapter-XXII/#">XXII&#58;</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Hee said, I goe sir, <b>and</b> went not.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Used to connect certain numbers: connecting units when they precede tens <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">not dated</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; connecting tens and units to hundreds, thousands etc. (now often omitted in US); to connect fractions to wholes. <span class="defdate">[from 10<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1863</b> November 19,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Abraham_Lincoln" class="extiw" title="w:Abraham Lincoln">Abraham Lincoln</a>,  <cite>Dedicatory Remarks</cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gettysburg_Address" class="extiw" title="w:Gettysburg Address">Gettysburg Address</a>)&#8206;<sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Gettysburg_Address_(Bliss_copy)">[1]</a></sup>, near <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gettysburg_National_Cemetery" class="extiw" title="w:Gettysburg National Cemetery">Soldiers' National Cemetery</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Library_of_Congress_Control_Number" class="extiw" title="w:Library of Congress Control Number">LCCN</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://lccn.loc.gov/n94107481">n94107481</a></small>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gettysburg_Address#Bliss_copy" class="extiw" title="w:Gettysburg Address">Bliss copy</a>, page 1:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Four score <b>and</b> seven years ago our fathers brought forth, on this continent, a new nation, conceived in Liberty, and dedicated to the proposition that all men are created equal.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1905</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upton_Sinclair" class="extiw" title="w:Upton Sinclair">Upton Sinclair</a>,  chapter <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/en:The_Jungle/Chapter_26">XXVI</a>, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Jungle" class="extiw" title="w:The Jungle">The Jungle</a></cite>, New York, N.Y.&#58; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Doubleday_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Doubleday (publisher)">Doubleday, Page &amp; Company</a>, published 26 February 1906, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/1150866071">1150866071</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In Chicago these latter were receiving, for the most part, eighteen <b>and</b> a half cents an hour, and the unions wished to make this the general wage for the next year.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1956</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dodie_Smith" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Dodie Smith">Dodie Smith</a>, (title):
<dl><dd>The One Hundred <b>and</b> One Dalmatians.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#colloquial" title="Appendix:Glossary">colloquial</a>&#32;or&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#literary" title="Appendix:Glossary">literary</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Used to connect more than two elements together in a chain, sometimes to stress the number of elements.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1599</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Julius_Caesar_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Julius Caesar (play)">The Tragedie of Iulius Cæsar</a>”, in  <cite>Mr. William Shakespeares Comedies, Histories, &amp; Tragedies<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Published According to the True Originall Copies.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London&#58; <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Printed by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act II, scene ii]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And these does she apply, for warnings <b>and</b> portents, / <b>And</b> euils imminent; and on her knee / Hath begg'd, that I will stay at home to day.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1939</b>, Langley, Ryerson &amp; Woolf, <i>The Wizard of Oz</i> (screenplay):
<dl><dd>Lions, <b>and</b> tigers, <b>and</b> bears! Oh, my!</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Connecting two identical elements, with implications of continued or infinite repetition. <span class="defdate">[from 10<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. Newly Translated out of the Originall Tongues: &amp; with the Former Translations Diligently Compared and Reuised, by His Maiesties Speciall Comandement. Appointed to be Read in Churches.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_James_Version" class="extiw" title="w:King James Version">King James Version</a>), London&#58; <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Imprinted at London by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barker_(printer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barker (printer)">Robert Barker</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="printer to the Kings Most Excellent Maiestie.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/964384981">964384981</a></small>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Psalms" class="extiw" title="w:Psalms">Psalms</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.kingjamesbibleonline.org/1611_Psalms-Chapter-CXLV/#">CXLV&#58;</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I will extol thee, my God, O king; and I will bless thy name for ever <b>and</b> ever.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2011</b>, Jonathan Watts, <i>The Guardian</i>, 18 March:
<dl><dd>He was at work in a nearby city when the tsunami struck. ‘As soon as I saw it, I called home. It rang <b>and</b> rang, but there was no answer.’</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Introducing a <a href="/wiki/parenthetical" title="parenthetical">parenthetical</a> or explanatory clause. <span class="defdate">[from 10<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1918</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_W._E._Russell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:George W. E. Russell">George W. E. Russell</a>, <i>Prime Ministers and Some Others</i>:
<dl><dd>The word "capable" occurs in Mr. Fisher's Bill, <b>and</b> rightly, because our mental and physical capacities are infinitely varied.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2008</b>, <i>The Guardian</i>, 29 Jan 2008:
<dl><dd>President Pervez Musharraf is undoubtedly sincere in his belief that he, <b>and</b> he alone, can save Pakistan from the twin perils of terrorism and anarchy.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Introducing the continuation of narration from a previous understood point; also used alone as a question: ‘and so what?’.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. Newly Translated out of the Originall Tongues: &amp; with the Former Translations Diligently Compared and Reuised, by His Maiesties Speciall Comandement. Appointed to be Read in Churches.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_James_Version" class="extiw" title="w:King James Version">King James Version</a>), London&#58; <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Imprinted at London by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barker_(printer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barker (printer)">Robert Barker</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="printer to the Kings Most Excellent Maiestie.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/964384981">964384981</a></small>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Revelation" class="extiw" title="w:Book of Revelation">Revelation</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.kingjamesbibleonline.org/1611_Revelation-Chapter-XIV/#">XIV&#58;</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b>And</b> I heard a voice from heaven, as the voice of many waters, and as the voice of a great thunder: and I heard the voice of harpers harping with their harps<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1860</b> December – <b>1861</b> August,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Dickens" class="extiw" title="w:Charles Dickens">Charles Dickens</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Expectations" class="extiw" title="w:Great Expectations">Great Expectations<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="&#91;...&#93; In Three Volumes">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, volume <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(please specify |volume=I, II, or III)</span>, London&#58; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chapman_%26_Hall" class="extiw" title="w:Chapman &amp; Hall">Chapman and Hall</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="193, Piccadilly.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, published October 1861, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/3359935">3359935</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">‘You take it smoothly now,’ said I, ‘but you were very serious last night, when you swore it was Death.’ ‘<b>And</b> so I swear it is Death,’ said he, putting his pipe back in his mouth<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1914</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saki" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Saki">Saki</a>, ‘The Lull’, <i>Beasts and Superbeasts</i>:
<dl><dd>‘<b>And</b>, Vera,’ added Mrs. Durmot, turning to her sixteen-year-old niece, ‘be careful what colour ribbon you wear in your hair<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>.’</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now&#32;regional&#32;or somewhat&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#colloquial" title="Appendix:Glossary">colloquial</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Used to connect two verbs where the second is dependent on the first: ‘<a href="/wiki/to" title="to">to</a>’. Used especially after <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/come#English" title="come">come</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/go#English" title="go">go</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/try#English" title="try">try</a></i>. <span class="defdate">[from 14<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1817</b> (date written)<b>&#8203;</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jane_Austen" class="extiw" title="w:Jane Austen">Jane Austen</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Raymond_Wilson_Chambers" class="extiw" title="w:Raymond Wilson Chambers">R[aymond] W[ilson] Chambers</a>, editor, <cite>Fragment of a Novel Written by Jane Austen, January–March 1817<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Now First Printed from the Manuscript">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></cite> &#91;<cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanditon" class="extiw" title="w:Sanditon">Sanditon</a></cite>&#93;, Oxford, Oxfordshire&#58; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oxford_University_Press" class="extiw" title="w:Oxford University Press">Clarendon Press</a>, published 1925, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/542356">542356</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Beyond paying her a few charming compliments and amusing her with gay conversation, had he done anything at all to try <b>and</b> gain her affection?</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1989</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Kelman" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:James Kelman">James Kelman</a>, <i>A Disaffection</i>:
<dl><dd>Remember <b>and</b> help yourself to the soup! called Gavin.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Introducing a <a href="/wiki/qualitative" title="qualitative">qualitative</a> difference between things having the same name; "as well as other". <span class="defdate">[from 16<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1936</b>, <i>The Labour Monthly</i>, vol. XVIII:
<dl><dd>Undoubtedly every party makes mistakes. But there are mistakes <b>and</b> mistakes.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1972</b>, <i>Esquire</i>, vol. LXXVIII:
<dl><dd>"There are managers <b>and</b> there are managers," he tells me. "I'm totally involved in every aspect of Nina's career."</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Used to combine numbers in <a href="/wiki/addition" title="addition">addition</a>; <a href="/wiki/plus" title="plus">plus</a> (with singular or plural verb). <span class="defdate">[from 17<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1791</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Boswell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:James Boswell">James Boswell</a>, <i>Life of Samuel Johnson</i>:
<dl><dd>‘Nobody attempts to dispute that two <b>and</b> two make four: but with contests concerning moral truth, human passions are generally mixed<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>.’</dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd>‘Can you do Addition?’ the White Queen asked. ‘What's one <b>and</b> one <b>and</b> one <b>and</b> one <b>and</b> one <b>and</b> one <b>and</b> one <b>and</b> one <b>and</b> one <b>and</b> one?’</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heading</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>Expressing a condition.</i>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now&#32;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dialectal" title="Appendix:Glossary">dialect</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/if" title="if">If</a>; provided that. <span class="defdate">[from 13<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1485</b>, Sir Thomas Malory, <i>Le Morte Darthur</i>, Book VII:
<dl><dd>"Where ys Sir Launcelot?" seyde King Arthure. "<b>And</b> he were here, he wolde nat grucche to do batayle for you."</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1526</b>,  &#91;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Tyndale" class="extiw" title="w:William Tyndale">William Tyndale</a>, transl.&#93;,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Testament" class="extiw" title="w:New Testament">The Newe Testamẽt<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="as it was Written and Caused to be Writtẽ by Them which Herde Yt. <ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <b>1595–1596</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Midsummer_Night%27s_Dream" class="extiw" title="w:A Midsummer Night&#39;s Dream">A Midsommer Nights Dreame</a>”, in  <cite>Mr. William Shakespeares Comedies, Histories, &amp; Tragedies: Published According to the True Originall Copies</cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London&#58; <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Printed by">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act I, scene ii]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I will roare you, <b>and</b> 'twere any Nightingale.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>

<dl><dd>As they will set an house on fire, <b>and</b> it were but to roast their eggs.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/mathematics" title="mathematics">mathematics</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/logic" title="logic">logic</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> connecting two <a href="/w/index.php?title=well_formed_formulas&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="well formed formulas (page does not exist)">well formed formulas</a> to create a well formed formula that requires the new formula to only be true when each of the two are true.</li></ol>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Quotations">Quotations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Quotations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<div class="NavFrame">
<div class="NavHead" style="text-align: left;">Usage notes</div>
<div class="NavContent derivedterms" style="text-align: left; column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;">
<ol><li>Beginning a sentence with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/and#English" title="and">and</a></i> or other coordinating conjunctions is considered incorrect by classical grammarians arguing that a coordinating conjunction at the start of a sentence has nothing to connect, but use of the word in this way is very common. The practice will be found in literature from Anglo-Saxon times onwards, especially as an aid to continuity in narrative and dialogue. The <i>OED</i> provides examples from the 9<sup>th</sup> century to the 19<sup>th</sup> century, including one from Shakespeare’s <i>King John:</i> “<i>Arthur</i>. Must you with hot Irons, burne out both mine eyes? <i>Hubert.</i> Young boy, I must. <i>Arthur</i>. And will you? <i>Hubert</i>. And I will.” It is also used for other rhetorical purposes, especially to denote surprise

<blockquote><p>(O John! and you have seen him! And are you really going?—1884 in <i>OED</i>) </p></blockquote>
<p>and sometimes just to introduce an improvised afterthought
</p>
<blockquote><p>(I’m going to swim. And don’t you dare watch—G. Butler, 1983)</p></blockquote>
It is, however, poor style to separate short statements into separate sentences when no special effect is needed: <i>I opened the door and I looked into the room</i> (not *<i>I opened the door. And I looked into the room</i>). Combining sentences or starting with <i>in addition</i> or <i>moreover</i> is preferred in formal writing.</li>

<li><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/and#English" title="and">And</a></i> is often omitted for contextual effects of various kinds, especially between sequences of descriptive adjectives which can be separated by commas or simply by spaces

<blockquote><p>(The teeming jerrybuilt dun-coloured traffic-ridden deafening city—Penelope Lively, 1987)</p></blockquote>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/and_all#English" title="and all">And all</a></i> is a well-established tag added to the end of a statement, as in
</p>
<blockquote><p>Isn’t it amazing? He has a Ph.D. and all—J. Shute, 1992</p></blockquote>
With the nominal meaning “also, besides, in addition”, the use has origins in dialect, as can be seen from the material from many regions given in the <i>English Dialect Dictionary</i> (often written in special ways, e.g., <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ano'</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">an'-all</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">an' a'</i>). In many of the examples it seems to lack any perceptible lexical meaning and to be just a rhythmical device to eke out a sentence.</li></ol>
</div></div>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Synonyms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">used to connect two similar words or phrases</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/as_well_as#English" title="as well as">as well as</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/together_with#English" title="together with">together with</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/in_addition_to#English" title="in addition to">in addition to</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="None" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/%26#English" title="&amp;">&amp;</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/%27n%27#English" title="&#39;n&#39;">'n'</a></span>, <span class="None" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/%2B#English" title="+">+</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in artist collaborations</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/x#English" title="x">x</a></span></li></ul>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">and</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ands#English" title="ands">ands</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/music" title="music">music</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;often informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In <a href="/wiki/rhythm" title="rhythm">rhythm</a>, the second half of a divided <a href="/wiki/beat" title="beat">beat</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2006</b>,  Goodwin, Gordon,  <cite>Gordon Goodwin's Big Phat Band: Trumpet</cite>, page 51:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The same goes for measure 42, when you begin the phrase on the <b>and</b> of 1, because that kind of lick can easily bog down the time.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/ande#Middle_English" title="ande">ande</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/anda#Old_English" title="anda">anda</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grudge, enmity, malice, envy, hatred, anger, zeal, annoyance, vexation; zeal; injury, mischief; fear, horror</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/andi#Old_Norse" title="andi">andi</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">breath, wind, spirit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; both from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anad%C3%B4" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anadô">*anadô</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">breath, anger, zeal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82enh%E2%82%81-" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂enh₁-">*h₂enh₁-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to breathe, blow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ahnd&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ahnd (page does not exist)">Ahnd</a>, <a href="/wiki/And#German" title="And">And</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">woe, grief</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/%C3%A5nde#Danish" title="ånde">ånde</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">breath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/wiki/anda#Swedish" title="anda">anda</a>, <a href="/wiki/ande#Swedish" title="ande">ande</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spirit, breath, wind, ingenuity, intellect</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href="/wiki/andi#Icelandic" title="andi">andi</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spirit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq"><a href="/wiki/%C3%ABnd%C3%AB#Albanian" title="ëndë">ëndë</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pleasure, delight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/animus#Latin" title="animus">animus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spirit, soul</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/onde#English" title="onde">onde</a></i>.
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">and</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ands#English" title="ands">ands</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_Kingdom" class="extiw" title="w:United Kingdom">UK</a>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dialectal" title="Appendix:Glossary">dialectal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/breath" title="breath">Breath</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_Kingdom" class="extiw" title="w:United Kingdom">UK</a>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dialectal" title="Appendix:Glossary">dialectal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sea_smoke" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Sea smoke">Sea smoke</a>; <a href="/w/index.php?title=steam_fog&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="steam fog (page does not exist)">steam fog</a>.</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Etymology 3">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/anden#Middle_English" title="anden">anden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/andian#Old_English" title="andian">andian</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be envious or jealous, envy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/anda#Old_Norse" title="anda">anda</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to breathe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; both from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anad%C5%8Dn%C4%85" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anadōną">*anadōną</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to breathe, sputter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/ahnden#German" title="ahnden">ahnden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to avenge, punish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/%C3%A5nde#Danish" title="ånde">ånde</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to breathe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/wiki/andas#Swedish" title="andas">andas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to breathe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href="/wiki/anda#Icelandic" title="anda">anda</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to breathe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See above.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Turkic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Turkic language">Proto-Turkic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="trk-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Turkic/%C4%80nt&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Turkic/Ānt (page does not exist)">*Ānt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">oath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Turkic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Turkic">Old Turkic</a></span> <i class="Orkh mention" lang="otk"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%F0%90%B0%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="𐰦 (page does not exist)">𐰦</a></i>&#8206; <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="otk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr"><a href="/wiki/ant#Turkish" title="ant">ant</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Danish">Danish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Danish">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/%C7%ABnd#Old_Norse" title="ǫnd">ǫnd</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anadz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anadz">*anadz</a></i>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/Ente#German" title="Ente">Ente</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/eend#Dutch" title="eend">eend</a></i>. The Germanic noun derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82%C3%A9nh%E2%82%82ts" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂énh₂ts">*h₂énh₂ts</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">duck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which is also the source of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/anas#Latin" title="anas">anas</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%CE%BD%E1%BF%86%CF%84%CF%84%CE%B1#Ancient_Greek" title="νῆττα">νῆττα</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nêtta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt"><a href="/wiki/antis#Lithuanian" title="antis">ántis</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa"><a href="/wiki/%E0%A4%86%E0%A4%A4%E0%A4%BF#Sanskrit" title="आति">आति</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ātí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_3">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Danish_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Danish pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/anˀ/</span>, <span class="IPA">[ænˀ]</span></li>
<li>Rhymes: <a href="/wiki/Rhymes:Danish/and" title="Rhymes:Danish/and"><span class="IPA">-and</span></a></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Estonian">Estonian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Estonian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From the root of <i class="Latn mention" lang="et"><a href="/wiki/andma#Estonian" title="andma">andma</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Finnish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Finnish language">Finnish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fi"><a href="/wiki/anti#Finnish" title="anti">anti</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Gothic">Gothic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Gothic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Romanization">Romanization</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Romanization">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="got">and</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Romanization of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Goth mention" lang="got"><a href="/wiki/%F0%90%8C%B0%F0%90%8C%BD%F0%90%8C%B3#Gothic" title="𐌰𐌽𐌳">𐌰𐌽𐌳</a></i></span></span></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Livonian">Livonian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Livonian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_4">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Courland</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="liv"><a href="/w/index.php?title=and%C3%B5&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="andõ (page does not exist)">andõ</a></span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Finnic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Finnic language">Proto-Finnic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fiu-fin-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Finnic/antadak" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Finnic/antadak">*antadak</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Uralic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Uralic language">Proto-Uralic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="urj-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Uralic/%C3%ABmta-" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Uralic/ëmta-">*ëmta-</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Middle_English">Middle English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Middle English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_5">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/annd#Middle_English" title="annd">annd</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/ant#Middle_English" title="ant">ant</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/an#Middle_English" title="an">an</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/en#Middle_English" title="en">en</a></span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/and#Old_English" title="and">and</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/ond#Old_English" title="ond">ond</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/end#Old_English" title="end">end</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/andi&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/andi (page does not exist)">*andi</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/andi" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/andi">*andi</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82%C3%A9nti" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂énti">*h₂énti</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_6">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Middle_English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Middle English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/and/</span></li>
