<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_2">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Conjunction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="enm">and</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/and#English" title="and">and</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/and#English" title="and">and</a></span> <a href="/wiki/then" title="then">then</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">connects two elements of a sentence</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <b>1200</b>,  Ormin,  “Dedication”, in  <cite>Ormulum</cite>, lines 1-4:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="enm">Nu broþerr Wallterr broþerr min / Affterr þe flæshess kinde / <b>⁊</b> broþerr min i Crisstendom / Þurrh  fulluhht <b>⁊</b> þurrh trowwþe <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span></span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Now, brother Walter, my brother / by way of blood relation / <b>and</b> my brother in Christendom / through baptising <b>and</b> through faith <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <b>1340</b>,  Dan Michel,  “Þe oþer Godes Heste”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ayenbite_of_Inwyt" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ayenbite of Inwyt">Ayenbite of Inwyt</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="enm">Ac þe ilke / þet zuereþ hidousliche be god / oþer by his halȝen / <b>and</b> him to-breȝþ / <b>and</b> zayþ him sclondres / þet ne byeþ naȝt to zigge: þe ilke zeneȝeþ dyadliche <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span></span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">But one who / hideously swears by God / or by his emissaries / <b>and</b> who tears him apart / <b>while</b> saying to him lies / that shouldn't be said: they sin grievously. <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <b>1380</b>,  <cite>Sir Firumbras</cite>, lines 4413-4414:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="enm">"Lordes", quaþ Richard, "Buþ noȝt agast, Ac holdeþ forþ ȝour way / <b>an</b> hast &amp; boldeliche doþ ȝour dede <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span>"</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">"Lords", said Richard, "Don't be frightened, but hold your way forwards / <b>and</b> quickly and boldy do your deed <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span>"</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <b>1395</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Wycliffe" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Wycliffe">John Wycliffe</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Purvey" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Purvey">John Purvey</a> [<i>et al.</i>], transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">Bible</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wycliffe_Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Wycliffe Bible">Wycliffite Bible (later version)</a>, MS Lich 10.)&#8206;<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://lichfield.ou.edu/wycliffe-new-testament/gallery">[2]</a></sup>, published c. 1410, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Book_of_Revelation" class="extiw" title="w:Book of Revelation">Apocalips</a>&#32;1&#58;8, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://static.lichfield.ou.edu/Wycliffe/_JPG-m-Watermarked/W117v-m.jpg">page 117v</a>&#59; republished as  <cite>Wycliffe's translation of the New Testament</cite>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lichfield" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lichfield">Lichfield</a>&#58; Bill Endres, 2010:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="enm">ȝhe amen / I am alpha <b>⁊</b> oo þe bigynnyng <b>⁊</b> þe ende ſeiþ þe loꝛd god þat is / <b>⁊</b> þat was. <b>⁊</b> that is to comynge almyȝti</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You, Amen! I am Alpha <b>and</b> O, the beginning <b>and</b> the end, says the Lord God; that is, that was, <b>and</b> that which will come, almighty.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1387–1400</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Geoffrey_Chaucer" class="extiw" title="w:Geoffrey Chaucer">Geoffrey Chaucer</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_Prologue" class="extiw" title="w:General Prologue">The Prologues</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Canterbury_Tales" class="extiw" title="w:The Canterbury Tales"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span>The Canterbury Tales<span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hengwrt_Chaucer" class="extiw" title="w:Hengwrt Chaucer">Hengwrt Chaucer</a>; <h2><span id="Norwegian_Bokm.C3.A5l"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Norwegian_Bokmål">Norwegian Bokmål</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Norwegian Bokmål">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Norwegian <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="no"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/no:ender" class="extiw" title="w:no:ender">ender</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/no:ender" class="extiw" title="w:no:ender">Wikipedia <sup>no</sup></a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/%C7%ABnd#Old_Norse" title="ǫnd">ǫnd</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anadz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anadz">*anadz</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82enh%E2%82%81-ti-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂enh₁-ti- (page does not exist)">*h₂enh₁-ti-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">duck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_7">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nb">and</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>definite singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nb"><a href="/wiki/anda#Norwegian_Bokmål" title="anda">anda</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nb"><a href="/wiki/anden#Norwegian_Bokmål" title="anden">anden</a></b>, <i>indefinite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nb"><a href="/wiki/ender#Norwegian_Bokmål" title="ender">ender</a></b>, <i>definite plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nb"><a href="/wiki/endene#Norwegian_Bokmål" title="endene">endene</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/duck#English" title="duck">duck</a></span></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/canard" title="canard">canard</a> (false or misleading report or story)</li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Norwegian_Nynorsk">Norwegian Nynorsk</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Norwegian Nynorsk">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_8">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Norwegian_Nynorsk_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Norwegian Nynorsk pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ɑnː/</span>, <span class="IPA">/ɑnd/</span> <small>(<a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:ANO#Pronunciation" class="mw-redirect" title="Wiktionary:ANO">examples</a> of pronunciation)</small></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Norwegian Nynorsk <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="nn"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nn:and" class="extiw" title="w:nn:and">and</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nn:and" class="extiw" title="w:nn:and">Wikipedia <sup>nn</sup></a></span></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/%C7%ABnd#Old_Norse" title="ǫnd">ǫnd</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anadz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anadz">*anadz</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82enh%E2%82%81-ti-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂enh₁-ti- (page does not exist)">*h₂enh₁-ti-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">duck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ennet#English" title="ennet">ennet</a></i>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_6">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_9">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anda&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anda (page does not exist)">*anda</a>, <a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/andi" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/andi">*andi</a></i>, probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82%C3%A9nti" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂énti">*h₂énti</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">facing opposite, near, in front of, before</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href="/wiki/and#Old_Frisian" title="and">and</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx"><a href="/wiki/endi#Old_Saxon" title="endi">endi</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/unti#Old_High_German" title="unti">unti</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/enn#Old_Norse" title="enn">enn</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_9">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Old_English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Old English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ɑnd/</span></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Old_Frisian">Old Frisian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=77" title="Edit section: Old Frisian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_7">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="ofs"><a href="/wiki/ande#Old_Frisian" title="ande">ande</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="ofs"><a href="/wiki/ende#Old_Frisian" title="ende">ende</a></span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_10">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=79" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/andi" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/andi">*andi</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82%C3%A9nti" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂énti">*h₂énti</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">facing opposite, near, in front of, before</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/and#Old_English" title="and">and</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx"><a href="/wiki/endi#Old_Saxon" title="endi">endi</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/unti#Old_High_German" title="unti">unti</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/enn#Old_Norse" title="enn">enn</a></i>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=84" title="Edit section: Pronoun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sga">and</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#third_person" title="Appendix:Glossary">third-person</a> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#singular_number" title="Appendix:Glossary">singular</a> <span class="inflection-of-conjoined"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#gender" title="Appendix:Glossary">masculine</a><span class="inflection-of-sep">/</span><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#gender" title="Appendix:Glossary">neuter</a></span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dative_case" title="Appendix:Glossary">dative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/hi#Old_Irish" title="hi">hi</a></i></span></span>: <a href="/wiki/in" title="in">in</a> <a href="/wiki/him" title="him">him</a>, <a href="/wiki/in" title="in">in</a> <a href="/wiki/it" title="it">it</a>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary">c.</a></i> <b>800–825</b>, Diarmait, Milan Glosses on the Psalms, published in <i>Thesaurus Palaeohibernicus</i> (reprinted 1987, Dublin Institute for Advanced Studies), edited and with translations by Whitley Stokes and John Strachan, vol.&#160;I, pp.&#160;7–483, Ml. 31<sup>b</sup>23
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="sga">in bélrai .i. is <b>and</b> atá gním tengad isind huiliu labramar-ni</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">of speech, i.e. the action of the tongue is in it, in all that we say</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=85" title="Edit section: Adverb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sga">and</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/there" title="there">there</a>
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary">c.</a></i> <b>850-875</b>, Turin Glosses and Scholia on St. Mark, published in <i>Thesaurus Palaeohibernicus</i> (reprinted 1987, Dublin Institute for Advanced Studies), edited and with translations by Whitley Stokes and John Strachan, vol.&#160;I, pp.&#160;484–94, Tur. 110c<sup></sup>
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="sga">Ba bés leusom do·bertis dá boc leu dochum tempuil, ⁊ no·léicthe indala n‑ái fon díthrub co pecad in popuil, ⁊ do·bertis maldachta foir, ⁊ n⟨o⟩·oircthe didiu <b>and</b> ó popul tar cenn a pecthae ind aile.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It was a custom with them that two he-goats were brought by them to the temple, and one of the two of them was let go to the wilderness with the sin of the people, and curses were put upon him, and thereupon the other was slain there by the people for their sins.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Scots">Scots</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=87" title="Edit section: Scots">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_5">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=88" title="Edit section: Conjunction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sco">and</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href="/wiki/an#Scots" title="an">an</a></i></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=89" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>While <i>and</i> is relatively often written due to English influence, it is seldom pronounced as such, making way for <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href="/wiki/an#Scots" title="an">an</a></i>. <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Swedish">Swedish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=91" title="Edit section: Swedish">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_11">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=92" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/%C7%ABnd#Old_Norse" title="ǫnd">ǫnd</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anadz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/anadz">*anadz</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82%C3%A9nh%E2%82%82t-" class="mw-redirect" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂énh₂t-">*h₂énh₂t-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">duck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_12">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=and&amp;action=edit&amp;section=106" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
